***гулянье.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нье</a> (22320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">guljánʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулянье.html>гуля́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>walk, walking; stroll</li>
<li>revelry, open-air merrymaking, outdoor fete; (<a href = vnd.unilang:поп.html>popular</a>) festival</li></ol>

***гулять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a> (1699)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">гуля́ць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huljácʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">гуляти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huljaty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">guljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погулять.html>погуля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to walk, to go for a walk, to stroll</li>
<li>to have time-off, to have free time</li>
<li>to make merry, to enjoy oneself, to carouse
<ol><li>to party</li></ol></li>
<li>to go with, to go out <i>with someone</i></li></ol>

***гумно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумно́</a> (24410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gumьno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gumnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гу́мна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гу́мен</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гумно.html>гумён</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> threshing-floor, cleared plot of land in farms on which stacks of grain are piled, accompanied by threshing and processing of grain</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">agriculture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> barn, shed for compressed grain</li>
<li>a minced oath form of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">gusar</i> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cursarius</i> <span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гусарский.html>гуса́рский</a> (26997)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусар.html>гуса́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gusár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусарский.html>гуса́рский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gusárskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hussar</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеница</a> (5591)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">юсеница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jusenica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">гу́сениця</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">húsenycja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">гъсе́ница</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gǎsénica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">гу̏сеница</i>/<span class="Latn" lang="sh">gȕsenica</span>/<span class="Cyrl" lang="sh">гу̏сјеница</span>/<span class="Latn" lang="sh">gȕsjenica</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">gosẹ̑nica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">housenka</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">husenica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish language">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">wąsienica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gąsienica</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">husańca</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">guseńca</i>. Probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ǫsěnica</i>. The initial <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">г</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">g</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>- is prothetic or by conflation with Common Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">гоущерица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gušterica</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lizard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ящерица.html>я́щерица</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jáščerica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), and is not related to Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусь.html>гусь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gusʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gúsenica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сеницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гусеница.html>гу́сениц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>caterpillar</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> caterpillar track</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gustój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густеть.html>густе́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gustétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загустеть.html>загусте́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">погусте́ть</b>)

***густо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>гу́сто</a> (3919)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫstъ</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">gust</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">гъст</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gǎst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Macedonian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Macedonian language">Macedonian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mk"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gust</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gęsty</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>гу́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gústo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thickly, densely</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>гу́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gústo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gustój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густо́й</a> (1450)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">густꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gustyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫstъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:густой.html>густо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gustój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick, dense <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">having a viscous consistency</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>rich, deep, heavy</li>
<li>dark, deep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a color</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***гуща.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a> (12887)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gušča</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫšča</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gǫstъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ща</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gúšča</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sediment, <i>(coffee)</i> grounds, <i>(beer)</i> lees, <i>soup</i> the body
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гадать.html>гада́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кофейный.html>кофе́йной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gadátʹ na koféjnoj gúšče</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to read the leaves, to make wild guesses (lit: tell fortunes by coffee grounds)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thicket
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>леса́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v gúšče lesá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the thick of the forest</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thick, centre, middle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́щу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:масса.html>ма́сс</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v sámuju <b>gúšču</b> mass</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the very midst of the masses</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гуща.html>гу́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:событие.html>собы́тий</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v samoj gúšče sobýtij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in the thick of things</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***да.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> (48)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*da</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>yes</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction_5">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>and (сочинительный, <a href = vnd.unilang:соединительный.html>соедини́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:союз.html>сою́з</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:император.html>импера́тору</a> Карлу <a href = vnd.unilang:великий.html>Вели́кому</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:недосуг.html>недосу́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писать</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On sam o sebé govoríl, što jemú, kak imperátoru Karlu Velikomu, nedosug učítʹsja čitátʹ <b>da</b> pisatʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He said of himself that he was like the Emperor Charlemagne, too busy to learn to read and write.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>but
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:граната.html>грана́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́мы</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Da</b> granáty u nevó ne toj sistémy!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">It's just - his grenades are the wrong caliber! (Quoted from <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_Sun_of_the_Desert" class="extiw" title="w:White Sun of the Desert">White Sun of the Desert</a> after antagonist fails to obtain grenades.)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Old-fashioned and usage.</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection_2">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>really
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расстаться.html>расста́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a>.<br />— <b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— My s nej rasstálisʹ užé kak mésjac nazád.<br />— <b>Da</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">“We broke up like a month ago.”<br />“Really?”</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>yes (<i>used to confirm that the person being addressed is listening</i>)</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_4">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">da</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>let + <i>verb</i></li>
<li>may + <i>verb</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:здравствовать.html>здра́вствует</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:республика.html>респу́блика</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>da</b> zdrávstvujet respúblika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">long live the republic</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бог.html>Бог</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>свет</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I skazál Box: <b>da</b> búdet svet.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">And God said: let there be light.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
